<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: 30px; text-indent: -0.5in; text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 18pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino; color: #ffffff; background-color: #808080;"><b><span style="line-height: 115%;">Spiritual Message for the Day – Jnana Yoga by Sri Swami Sivananada</span></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" style="margin-left: 30px; text-indent: -0.5in; text-align: center;"><strong style="text-indent: -0.5in;"><span style="font-family: book antiqua,palatino; font-size: 12pt; color: #3366ff;"><span style="line-height: 115%;"><span style="color: #0000ff;">Baba Times Digest© | 19 May 2015 16.34 EST | New York Edition</span></span></span></strong></p>
<hr />
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Jnana Yoga<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>Divine Life Society Publication: </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/amrita.htm#_VPID_8"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Amrita Gita</b></span></a></span><b> by Sri Swami Sivananda<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>
<ol style="margin-top: 0in;" start="1" type="1">
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">There is an Atman or soul independent of body and mind. This soul is immortal, unchanging and infinite. Realise this Atman and be free. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This Atman is Satchidananda (Existence-Absolute, Consciousness-Absolute, and Bliss-Absolute). It exists in the past, present and future. So it is Sat. It is pure or Absolute Consciousness without any thought. So it is Chit. It is absolute Bliss. So it is Ananda. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">The unreal body perishes, but the Atman or the indweller is Immortal. So, you should not grieve when anyone dies. In essence everyone is Immortal Atman. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This Atman cannot be hurt by anyone. It is subtle, all-pervading. It is the Innermost Self of all. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This Atman is birthless, deathless, changeless. When the body is killed, He is not killed. Therefore grieve not, lament not, regret not. Be always cheerful. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Fire cannot burn this Atman, sword cannot pierce this Atman, bomb cannot destroy this Atman, machine-guns cannot kill this Atman. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This Atman is eternal, immovable, secondless, self-existent, self-centred. Therefore, knowing this to be such, thou shouldst not grieve, when your father, mother, son, wife or relative dies. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This perishable body will certainly pass away. Indweller can never perish. Thou art the immortal soul. Therefore, over the inevitable thou shalt not grieve. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Brahman or Atman is beyond the reach of the mind and speech. He is beyond logic, reason, mental process, science. He must be realised through meditation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">You cannot deny or doubt your existence. You always feel that you exist. This existence is Atman or your own Self. The knower of the doubt or denier always exists. That knower is your own Atman. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">In dream you are distinct from the physical body. In deep sleep, you are distinct from the body and the mind. You enjoy peace and bliss in deep sleep. This proves that you are neither body nor mind, but you are All-Blissful Soul. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">There is only one Reality or Truth. That is Brahman or Atman. All appearances are unreal. They are the effects of Maya, the illusory power of Brahman. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Behold the one Immortal Atman in all names and forms. This alone is correct perception. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Ignorance is the cause for pain and sorrow. Annihilate this ignorance through Brahma Jnana. All miseries will come to an end. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This Atman is beyond time, space, causation. Time, space, causation are mental creation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Just as snake is superimposed on the rope, this world, and the body are superimposed on Brahman. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Bring a light, the snake vanishes; rope alone remains. Attain Illumination, this world and this body vanish. Atman alone remains. That Atman thou art. Tat Tvam Asi. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">I-ness and mine-ness, agency and enjoyership bind you to the Samsara. Destroy these notions. Identify yourself with the Atman which is non-doer, non-enjoyer. You will attain Immortality and eternal Bliss. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Sensual pleasure is only pain. It is momentary mental excitement, momentary sensation of flesh, momentary itching and scratching of the senses. You can have eternal bliss in your own Inner Atman alone. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Enquire ‘Who am I?’ Deny or sublate the limiting adjuncts (body, mind, etc.); know the Self and be free. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Constantly think of the Immortal, all-pervading Atman. Give up thinking of body. You will attain Self-realisation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">You are ever free. You are already free. Moksha is not a thing to be attained. You will have to know that you are Atman, that you are free. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Destroy the Vasanas, subtle desires, and Trishnas, cravings. This will lead to the annihilation of the mind. Destruction of the mind will lead to the attainment of Brahma Jnana or wisdom of the Self. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">This world is illusory. Brahman alone is real. You are identical with Brahman. Realise this and be free. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">The liberated sage is ever blissful. He rests in his own Satchidananda Svaroopa. He is free from egoism, lust, hatred, greed, anger and the pairs of opposites. He has equal vision and balanced mind. He is Brahman Himself. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">OM is the symbol of Brahman. OM is your real name. Meditate on Om with Bhava and its meaning. You will attain Self-realisation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">“I am the All-pervading, Immortal Soul. I am Pure Consciousness. I am Satchidananda Svaroopa. I am witness or Sakshi.”—These are the formulas for constant meditation and assertion. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Equip yourself with the Four Means. Hear the Srutis, reflect and meditate. You will attain Self-realisation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Thou art not this perishable body. Thou art not this changing mind. Thou art all-pervading, immortal, infinite, changeless Soul or Atman. Realise this and roam about happily. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">Watch the breath. It sings Soham, ‘So’ during inhalation and ‘Ham’, during exhalation. It reminds you ‘I am He’. Meditate on ‘Soham’ and attain Self-realisation. </span></li>
<li class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; mso-list: l0 level1 lfo1; tab-stops: list .5in;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;">‘I am body. I act. I enjoy. She is my wife. He is my son. This is mine.’—This is bondage. ‘I am Immortal Soul. I am non-actor, non-enjoyer. She is my soul. Nothing is mine.’—This is freedom. </span></li>
</ol>
<p align="center" style="margin: 0in; margin-bottom: .0001pt; text-align: center;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><b>THUS ENDS JNANA YOGA OR</b> <br /> <b>THE YOGA OF THE WISDOM OF THE SELF</b> <o:p></o:p></span></p>
<p class="MsoNoSpacing" align="center" style="text-align: center;">&nbsp;</p>
<p class="MsoNormal" style="margin-bottom: .0001pt; line-height: normal; tab-stops: 115.5pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"><span class="MsoHyperlink"><b>Excerpts from: </b></span><b>Jnana<a name="_GoBack"></a> Yoga &nbsp;- </b><span style="color: #0000ff;"><a href="http://www.dlshq.org/download/amrita.htm#_VPID_8"><span style="color: #0000ff;"><b>Amrita Gita</b></span></a></span></span><b><span style="font-size: 9.0pt;"><span style="font-size: 12pt; font-family: 'book antiqua', palatino;"> by Sri Swami Sivananda</span><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

   UnhideWhenUsed="false" Name="Light Shading Accent 2"/>
